Summary:
## 1. Primary Request and Intent:

The user's primary requests were:
1. **Load session logs** (`/sl` command) for continuity from previous sessions
2. **Switch to full Docker mode** - but first fix the `--switch-to-docker` command to handle Docker Desktop not running. The script must automatically start Docker Desktop and ensure safe, robust transitions.
3. **Final request**: Investigate Docker Desktop stability issues by checking settings, Activity Monitor, logs, trying reset, and checking for updates.

## 2. Key Technical Concepts:

- **Docker Mode Transition System**: Safe switching between native and Docker deployment modes with rollback capability
- **Process State Manager (PSM)**: Service registration and monitoring system
- **Health Monitoring with SIGUSR2/SIGUSR1**: Pause/resume signals for health monitors during transitions
- **Port binding conflicts**: Native services vs Docker containers competing for same ports
- **Container naming conventions**: Native mode uses `constraint-monitor-*`, `code-graph-rag-*` vs Docker compose uses `coding-*`
- **Docker Desktop auto-start on macOS**: Using `open -a "Docker"` and polling `docker ps`
- **Health check timeouts**: Docker `start_period: 120s` vs script timeout coordination

## 3. Files and Code Sections:

### `<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>cker-mode-transition.js`
**Why important**: This is the main file implementing the `--switch-to-docker` and `--switch-to-native` commands.

**Key additions:**

```javascript
// Health check timeout (must exceed Docker's start_period of 120s for coding-services)
const HEALTH_CHECK_TIMEOUT_MS = 150 * 1000;

// Docker startup timeout (wait for Docker Desktop to start)
const DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS = 45 * 1000;
```

```javascript
/**
 * Check if Docker daemon is ready (not just client)
 */
isDockerDaemonReady() {
  try {
    execSync('docker ps', { encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe' });
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Ensure Docker Desktop is running before attempting Docker operations
 * Mirrors the ensure_docker_running() logic from launch-claude.sh
 */
async ensureDockerRunning() {
  // Quick check if already running
  if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
    this.log('Docker daemon is already running');
    return true;
  }

  this.log('Docker daemon not running - attempting to start Docker Desktop...');

  // Check for stale Docker processes
  try {
    const psOutput = execSync('ps aux | grep -c "[c]om.docker.backend" || echo "0"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim();

    if (parseInt(psOutput) > 0) {
      this.log('Found stale Docker processes - force restarting...', 'warn');
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "Docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "com.docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      await this.sleep(2000);
    }
  } catch {
    // Ignore errors from ps/pkill
  }

  // Try to start Docker Desktop (macOS)
  const dockerAppPath = '/Applications/Docker.app';
  try {
    await fs.access(dockerAppPath);
  } catch {
    this.log('Docker Desktop not found at /Applications/Docker.app', 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Start Docker Desktop
  this.log('Starting Docker Desktop...');
  try {
    execSync('open -a "Docker"', { stdio: 'pipe' });
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Failed to launch Docker Desktop: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Wait for Docker daemon to become ready
  this.log(`Waiting for Docker daemon (max ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS / 1000} seconds)...`);
  const startTime = Date.now();

  while (Date.now() - startTime < DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS) {
    if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
      const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - startTime) / 1000);
      this.log(`Docker daemon ready after ${elapsed} seconds`);
      return true;
    }
    await this.sleep(1000);
  }

  this.log(`Docker daemon not ready after ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS/1000} seconds`, 'error');
  return false;
}
```

**Updated `servicesToStop` array:**
```javascript
const servicesToStop = [
  'system-health-dashboard-frontend',
  'system-health-dashboard-api',
  'vkb-server',
  'semantic-analysis-server',
  'constraint-monitor',
  'transcript-monitor',
  'live-logging-coordinator'
];
```

**Updated container stopping logic (BEFORE port killing):**
```javascript
// FIRST: Stop standalone Docker containers that may have been started by native mode services
if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
  this.log('Stopping standalone Docker containers from native mode...');

  const containerPatterns = [
    'constraint-monitor-',  // Redis, Qdrant from constraint monitor
    'code-graph-rag-',      // Memgraph, Lab from code-graph-rag
    'coding-'               // Any coding- prefixed containers
  ];

  try {
    const runningContainers = execSync('docker ps --format "{{.Names}}"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim().split('\n').filter(Boolean);

    for (const containerName of runningContainers) {
      if (containerPatterns.some(pattern => containerName.startsWith(pattern))) {
        this.log(`Stopping standalone container: ${containerName}...`);
        execSync(`docker stop ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe', timeout: 15000
        });
        execSync(`docker rm ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe'
        });
        this.log(`Stopped ${containerName}`);
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Warning: Could not list/stop containers: ${error.message}`, 'warn');
  }

  await this.sleep(2000);  // Give Docker time to release port bindings
}
```

**Updated port killing (only native ports):**
```javascript
// THEN: Release any remaining ports (non-Docker native processes)
const nativePorts = [
  8080,   // VKB Server
  3032,   // Health Dashboard HTTP
  3033,   // Health Dashboard WebSocket
  3847,   // Browser Access SSE
  3848,   // Semantic Analysis SSE
  3849,   // Constraint Monitor SSE
  3850    // Code-Graph-RAG SSE
];
```

**Updated `transition()` method - early Docker check:**
```javascript
try {
  // CRITICAL: If transitioning TO Docker, ensure Docker is running BEFORE stopping native services
  if (targetMode === 'docker') {
    this.log('Ensuring Docker is available for transition...');
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - cannot proceed with transition');
    }
  }
  // ... rest of transition logic
}
```

**Updated `startDockerContainers()` - added Docker check:**
```javascript
async startDockerContainers() {
  this.log('Starting Docker containers...');
  await this.updateLockStatus('starting_docker');

  try {
    // First ensure Docker Desktop is running
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - please start Docker Desktop');
    }
    // ... rest of method
  }
}
```

### `<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ker-compose.yml`
**Why important**: Shows the ports and health check configuration for Docker mode:
- `coding-services`: ports 8080, 3032, 3033, 3847-3850, start_period 120s
- `coding-qdrant`: ports 6333-6334
- `coding-redis`: port 6379  
- `coding-memgraph`: ports 7687, 3100

## 4. Errors and Fixes:

1. **Port 3033 already in use (System Health Dashboard API)**
   - Fix: Added `system-health-dashboard-frontend` and `system-health-dashboard-api` to `servicesToStop` and `scriptPatterns`

2. **Port 3100 already in use (Memgraph Lab)**
   - Fix: Added logic to stop standalone containers matching patterns `constraint-monitor-*`, `code-graph-rag-*`

3. **Port 6379 already in use (Redis) - Docker crashing**
   - Root cause: Killing processes on Docker-owned ports was killing container processes, confusing Docker
   - Fix: Moved container stopping BEFORE port killing; only kill native service ports, not Docker-owned ports

4. **Docker daemon not available during `stopNativeServices()`**
   - Root cause: Docker check happened too late
   - Fix: Added `ensureDockerRunning()` call at START of `transition()` method

5. **Health check timeout after 60s**
   - Root cause: Docker's `start_period: 120s` > script's 60s timeout
   - Fix: Increased `HEALTH_CHECK_TIMEOUT_MS` from 60000 to 150000ms

6. **Docker Desktop repeatedly crashing**
   - Status: UNRESOLVED - Docker Desktop stability issue on user's machine, not script issue

## 5. Problem Solving:

**Solved:**
- Docker auto-start logic implemented
- Proper ordering of operations (containers before ports)
- Correct identification of which ports are Docker-owned vs native
- Extended health check timeouts

**Ongoing:**
- Docker Desktop stability - keeps crashing during operations (system issue, not script issue)

Summary:
## 1. Primary Request and Intent:

The user's primary requests were:
1. **Load session logs** (`/sl` command) for continuity from previous sessions
2. **Switch to full Docker mode** - but first fix the `--switch-to-docker` command to handle Docker Desktop not running. The script must automatically start Docker Desktop and ensure safe, robust transitions.
3. **Final request**: Investigate Docker Desktop stability issues by checking settings, Activity Monitor, logs, trying reset, and checking for updates.

## 2. Key Technical Concepts:

- **Docker Mode Transition System**: Safe switching between native and Docker deployment modes with rollback capability
- **Process State Manager (PSM)**: Service registration and monitoring system
- **Health Monitoring with SIGUSR2/SIGUSR1**: Pause/resume signals for health monitors during transitions
- **Port binding conflicts**: Native services vs Docker containers competing for same ports
- **Container naming conventions**: Native mode uses `constraint-monitor-*`, `code-graph-rag-*` vs Docker compose uses `coding-*`
- **Docker Desktop auto-start on macOS**: Using `open -a "Docker"` and polling `docker ps`
- **Health check timeouts**: Docker `start_period: 120s` vs script timeout coordination

## 3. Files and Code Sections:

### `<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>cker-mode-transition.js`
**Why important**: This is the main file implementing the `--switch-to-docker` and `--switch-to-native` commands.

**Key additions:**

```javascript
// Health check timeout (must exceed Docker's start_period of 120s for coding-services)
const HEALTH_CHECK_TIMEOUT_MS = 150 * 1000;

// Docker startup timeout (wait for Docker Desktop to start)
const DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS = 45 * 1000;
```

```javascript
/**
 * Check if Docker daemon is ready (not just client)
 */
isDockerDaemonReady() {
  try {
    execSync('docker ps', { encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe' });
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Ensure Docker Desktop is running before attempting Docker operations
 * Mirrors the ensure_docker_running() logic from launch-claude.sh
 */
async ensureDockerRunning() {
  // Quick check if already running
  if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
    this.log('Docker daemon is already running');
    return true;
  }

  this.log('Docker daemon not running - attempting to start Docker Desktop...');

  // Check for stale Docker processes
  try {
    const psOutput = execSync('ps aux | grep -c "[c]om.docker.backend" || echo "0"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim();

    if (parseInt(psOutput) > 0) {
      this.log('Found stale Docker processes - force restarting...', 'warn');
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "Docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "com.docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      await this.sleep(2000);
    }
  } catch {
    // Ignore errors from ps/pkill
  }

  // Try to start Docker Desktop (macOS)
  const dockerAppPath = '/Applications/Docker.app';
  try {
    await fs.access(dockerAppPath);
  } catch {
    this.log('Docker Desktop not found at /Applications/Docker.app', 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Start Docker Desktop
  this.log('Starting Docker Desktop...');
  try {
    execSync('open -a "Docker"', { stdio: 'pipe' });
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Failed to launch Docker Desktop: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Wait for Docker daemon to become ready
  this.log(`Waiting for Docker daemon (max ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS / 1000} seconds)...`);
  const startTime = Date.now();

  while (Date.now() - startTime < DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS) {
    if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
      const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - startTime) / 1000);
      this.log(`Docker daemon ready after ${elapsed} seconds`);
      return true;
    }
    await this.sleep(1000);
  }

  this.log(`Docker daemon not ready after ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS/1000} seconds`, 'error');
  return false;
}
```

**Updated `servicesToStop` array:**
```javascript
const servicesToStop = [
  'system-health-dashboard-frontend',
  'system-health-dashboard-api',
  'vkb-server',
  'semantic-analysis-server',
  'constraint-monitor',
  'transcript-monitor',
  'live-logging-coordinator'
];
```

**Updated container stopping logic (BEFORE port killing):**
```javascript
// FIRST: Stop standalone Docker containers that may have been started by native mode services
if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
  this.log('Stopping standalone Docker containers from native mode...');

  const containerPatterns = [
    'constraint-monitor-',  // Redis, Qdrant from constraint monitor
    'code-graph-rag-',      // Memgraph, Lab from code-graph-rag
    'coding-'               // Any coding- prefixed containers
  ];

  try {
    const runningContainers = execSync('docker ps --format "{{.Names}}"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim().split('\n').filter(Boolean);

    for (const containerName of runningContainers) {
      if (containerPatterns.some(pattern => containerName.startsWith(pattern))) {
        this.log(`Stopping standalone container: ${containerName}...`);
        execSync(`docker stop ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe', timeout: 15000
        });
        execSync(`docker rm ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe'
        });
        this.log(`Stopped ${containerName}`);
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Warning: Could not list/stop containers: ${error.message}`, 'warn');
  }

  await this.sleep(2000);  // Give Docker time to release port bindings
}
```

**Updated port killing (only native ports):**
```javascript
// THEN: Release any remaining ports (non-Docker native processes)
const nativePorts = [
  8080,   // VKB Server
  3032,   // Health Dashboard HTTP
  3033,   // Health Dashboard WebSocket
  3847,   // Browser Access SSE
  3848,   // Semantic Analysis SSE
  3849,   // Constraint Monitor SSE
  3850    // Code-Graph-RAG SSE
];
```

**Updated `transition()` method - early Docker check:**
```javascript
try {
  // CRITICAL: If transitioning TO Docker, ensure Docker is running BEFORE stopping native services
  if (targetMode === 'docker') {
    this.log('Ensuring Docker is available for transition...');
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - cannot proceed with transition');
    }
  }
  // ... rest of transition logic
}
```

**Updated `startDockerContainers()` - added Docker check:**
```javascript
async startDockerContainers() {
  this.log('Starting Docker containers...');
  await this.updateLockStatus('starting_docker');

  try {
    // First ensure Docker Desktop is running
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - please start Docker Desktop');
    }
    // ... rest of method
  }
}
```

### `<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ker-compose.yml`

- `coding-services`: ports 8080, 3032, 3033, 3847-3850, start_period 120s
- `coding-qdrant`: ports 6333-6334
- `coding-redis`: port 6379  
- `coding-memgraph`: ports 7687, 3100

## 4. Errors and Fixes:

1. **Port 3033 already in use (System Health Dashboard API)**
   - Fix: Added `system-health-dashboard-frontend` and `system-health-dashboard-api` to `servicesToStop` and `scriptPatterns`

2. **Port 3100 already in use (Memgraph Lab)**
   - Fix: Added logic to stop standalone containers matching patterns `constraint-monitor-*`, `code-graph-rag-*`

3. **Port 6379 already in use (Redis) - Docker crashing**
   - Root cause: Killing processes on Docker-owned ports was killing container processes, confusing Docker
   - Fix: Moved container stopping BEFORE port killing; only kill native service ports, not Docker-owned ports

4. **Docker daemon not available during `stopNativeServices()`**
   - Root cause: Docker check happened too late
   - Fix: Added `ensureDockerRunning()` call at START of `transition()` method

5. **Health check timeout after 60s**
   - Root cause: Docker's `start_period: 120s` > script's 60s timeout
   - Fix: Increased `HEALTH_CHECK_TIMEOUT_MS` from 60000 to 150000ms

6. **Docker Desktop repeatedly crashing**
   - Status: UNRESOLVED - Docker Desktop stability issue on user's machine, not script issue

## 5. Problem Solving:

**Solved:**
- Docker auto-start logic implemented
- Proper ordering of operations (containers before ports)
- Correct identification of which ports are Docker-owned vs native
- Extended health check timeouts

**Ongoing:**
- Docker Desktop stability - keeps crashing during operations (system issue, not script issue)

```javascript
/**
 * Check if Docker daemon is ready (not just client)
 */
isDockerDaemonReady() {
  try {
    execSync('docker ps', { encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe' });
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Ensure Docker Desktop is running before attempting Docker operations
 * Mirrors the ensure_docker_running() logic from launch-claude.sh
 */
async ensureDockerRunning() {
  // Quick check if already running
  if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
    this.log('Docker daemon is already running');
    return true;
  }

  this.log('Docker daemon not running - attempting to start Docker Desktop...');

  // Check for stale Docker processes
  try {
    const psOutput = execSync('ps aux | grep -c "[c]om.docker.backend" || echo "0"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim();

    if (parseInt(psOutput) > 0) {
      this.log('Found stale Docker processes - force restarting...', 'warn');
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "Docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "com.docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      await this.sleep(2000);
    }
  } catch {
    // Ignore errors from ps/pkill
  }

  // Try to start Docker Desktop (macOS)
  const dockerAppPath = '/Applications/Docker.app';
  try {
    await fs.access(dockerAppPath);
  } catch {
    this.log('Docker Desktop not found at /Applications/Docker.app', 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Start Docker Desktop
  this.log('Starting Docker Desktop...');
  try {
    execSync('open -a "Docker"', { stdio: 'pipe' });
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Failed to launch Docker Desktop: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Wait for Docker daemon to become ready
  this.log(`Waiting for Docker daemon (max ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS / 1000} seconds)...`);
  const startTime = Date.now();

  while (Date.now() - startTime < DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS) {
    if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
      const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - startTime) / 1000);
      this.log(`Docker daemon ready after ${elapsed} seconds`);
      return true;
    }
    await this.sleep(1000);
  }

  this.log(`Docker daemon not ready after ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS/1000} seconds`, 'error');
  return false;
}

## 1. Primary Request and Intent:

The user's primary requests were:
1. **Load session logs** (`/sl` command) for continuity from previous sessions

## 2. Key Technical Concepts:

- **Docker Mode Transition System**: Safe switching between native and Docker deployment modes with rollback capability
- **Process State Manager (PSM)**: Service registration and monitoring system
- **Health Monitoring with SIGUSR2/SIGUSR1**: Pause/resume signals for health monitors during transitions
- **Port binding conflicts**: Native services vs Docker containers competing for same ports
- **Container naming conventions**: Native mode uses `constraint-monitor-*`, `code-graph-rag-*` vs Docker compose uses `coding-*`
- **Docker Desktop auto-start on macOS**: Using `open -a "Docker"` and polling `docker ps`
- **Health check timeouts**: Docker `start_period: 120s` vs script timeout coordination

## 3. Files and Code Sections:

### `<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>cker-mode-transition.js`
**Why important**: This is the main file implementing the `--switch-to-docker` and `--switch-to-native` commands.

**Key additions:**

```javascript
// Health check timeout (must exceed Docker's start_period of 120s for coding-services)
const HEALTH_CHECK_TIMEOUT_MS = 150 * 1000;

// Docker startup timeout (wait for Docker Desktop to start)
const DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS = 45 * 1000;
```

```javascript
/**
 * Check if Docker daemon is ready (not just client)
 */
isDockerDaemonReady() {
  try {
    execSync('docker ps', { encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe' });
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Ensure Docker Desktop is running before attempting Docker operations
 * Mirrors the ensure_docker_running() logic from launch-claude.sh
 */
async ensureDockerRunning() {
  // Quick check if already running
  if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
    this.log('Docker daemon is already running');
    return true;
  }

  this.log('Docker daemon not running - attempting to start Docker Desktop...');

  // Check for stale Docker processes
  try {
    const psOutput = execSync('ps aux | grep -c "[c]om.docker.backend" || echo "0"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim();

    if (parseInt(psOutput) > 0) {
      this.log('Found stale Docker processes - force restarting...', 'warn');
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "Docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "com.docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      await this.sleep(2000);
    }
  } catch {
    // Ignore errors from ps/pkill
  }

  // Try to start Docker Desktop (macOS)
  const dockerAppPath = '/Applications/Docker.app';
  try {
    await fs.access(dockerAppPath);
  } catch {
    this.log('Docker Desktop not found at /Applications/Docker.app', 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Start Docker Desktop
  this.log('Starting Docker Desktop...');
  try {
    execSync('open -a "Docker"', { stdio: 'pipe' });
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Failed to launch Docker Desktop: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Wait for Docker daemon to become ready
  this.log(`Waiting for Docker daemon (max ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS / 1000} seconds)...`);
  const startTime = Date.now();

  while (Date.now() - startTime < DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS) {
    if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
      const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - startTime) / 1000);
      this.log(`Docker daemon ready after ${elapsed} seconds`);
      return true;
    }
    await this.sleep(1000);
  }

  this.log(`Docker daemon not ready after ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS/1000} seconds`, 'error');
  return false;
}
```

**Updated `servicesToStop` array:**
```javascript
const servicesToStop = [
  'system-health-dashboard-frontend',
  'system-health-dashboard-api',
  'vkb-server',
  'semantic-analysis-server',
  'constraint-monitor',
  'transcript-monitor',
  'live-logging-coordinator'
];
```

**Updated container stopping logic (BEFORE port killing):**
```javascript
// FIRST: Stop standalone Docker containers that may have been started by native mode services
if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
  this.log('Stopping standalone Docker containers from native mode...');

  const containerPatterns = [
    'constraint-monitor-',  // Redis, Qdrant from constraint monitor
    'code-graph-rag-',      // Memgraph, Lab from code-graph-rag
    'coding-'               // Any coding- prefixed containers
  ];

  try {
    const runningContainers = execSync('docker ps --format "{{.Names}}"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim().split('\n').filter(Boolean);

    for (const containerName of runningContainers) {
      if (containerPatterns.some(pattern => containerName.startsWith(pattern))) {
        this.log(`Stopping standalone container: ${containerName}...`);
        execSync(`docker stop ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe', timeout: 15000
        });
        execSync(`docker rm ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe'
        });
        this.log(`Stopped ${containerName}`);
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Warning: Could not list/stop containers: ${error.message}`, 'warn');
  }

  await this.sleep(2000);  // Give Docker time to release port bindings
}
```

**Updated port killing (only native ports):**
```javascript
// THEN: Release any remaining ports (non-Docker native processes)
const nativePorts = [
  8080,   // VKB Server
  3032,   // Health Dashboard HTTP
  3033,   // Health Dashboard WebSocket
  3847,   // Browser Access SSE
  3848,   // Semantic Analysis SSE
  3849,   // Constraint Monitor SSE
  3850    // Code-Graph-RAG SSE
];
```

**Updated `transition()` method - early Docker check:**
```javascript
try {
  // CRITICAL: If transitioning TO Docker, ensure Docker is running BEFORE stopping native services
  if (targetMode === 'docker') {
    this.log('Ensuring Docker is available for transition...');
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - cannot proceed with transition');
    }
  }
  // ... rest of transition logic
}
```

**Updated `startDockerContainers()` - added Docker check:**
```javascript
async startDockerContainers() {
  this.log('Starting Docker containers...');
  await this.updateLockStatus('starting_docker');

  try {
    // First ensure Docker Desktop is running
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - please start Docker Desktop');
    }
    // ... rest of method
  }
}
```

3. **Port 6379 already in use (Redis) - Docker crashing**

   - Fix: Moved container stopping BEFORE port killing; only kill native service ports, not Docker-owned ports

4. **Docker daemon not available during `stopNativeServices()`**
   - Root cause: Docker check happened too late
   - Fix: Added `ensureDockerRunning()` call at START of `transition()` method

5. **Health check timeout after 60s**
   - Root cause: Docker's `start_period: 120s` > script's 60s timeout
   - Fix: Increased `HEALTH_CHECK_TIMEOUT_MS` from 60000 to 150000ms

6. **Docker Desktop repeatedly crashing**
   - Status: UNRESOLVED - Docker Desktop stability issue on user's machine, not script issue

 */

    execSync('docker ps', { encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe' });
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }

/**
 * Ensure Docker Desktop is running before attempting Docker operations
 * Mirrors the ensure_docker_running() logic from launch-claude.sh
 */
async ensureDockerRunning() {
  // Quick check if already running
  if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
    this.log('Docker daemon is already running');
    return true;
  }

  this.log('Docker daemon not running - attempting to start Docker Desktop...');

  // Check for stale Docker processes
  try {
    const psOutput = execSync('ps aux | grep -c "[c]om.docker.backend" || echo "0"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim();

    if (parseInt(psOutput) > 0) {
      this.log('Found stale Docker processes - force restarting...', 'warn');
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "Docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "com.docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      await this.sleep(2000);
    }
  } catch {
    // Ignore errors from ps/pkill
  }

  // Try to start Docker Desktop (macOS)
  const dockerAppPath = '/Applications/Docker.app';
  try {
    await fs.access(dockerAppPath);
  } catch {
    this.log('Docker Desktop not found at /Applications/Docker.app', 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Start Docker Desktop
  this.log('Starting Docker Desktop...');
  try {
    execSync('open -a "Docker"', { stdio: 'pipe' });
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Failed to launch Docker Desktop: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Wait for Docker daemon to become ready
  this.log(`Waiting for Docker daemon (max ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS / 1000} seconds)...`);
  const startTime = Date.now();

  while (Date.now() - startTime < DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS) {
    if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
      const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - startTime) / 1000);
      this.log(`Docker daemon ready after ${elapsed} seconds`);
      return true;
    }
    await this.sleep(1000);
  }

  this.log(`Docker daemon not ready after ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS/1000} seconds`, 'error');
  return false;
}

          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe'
        });
        this.log(`Stopped ${containerName}`);
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Warning: Could not list/stop containers: ${error.message}`, 'warn');
  }

  await this.sleep(2000);  // Give Docker time to release port bindings
}
```

**Updated port killing (only native ports):**
```javascript

const nativePorts = [
  8080,   // VKB Server

  3847,   // Browser Access SSE
  3848,   // Semantic Analysis SSE
  3849,   // Constraint Monitor SSE
  3850    // Code-Graph-RAG SSE
];
```

```javascript
try {
  // CRITICAL: If transitioning TO Docker, ensure Docker is running BEFORE stopping native services
  if (targetMode === 'docker') {
    this.log('Ensuring Docker is available for transition...');
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - cannot proceed with transition');
    }
  }
  // ... rest of transition logic
}
```

```javascript
async startDockerContainers() {
  this.log('Starting Docker containers...');
  await this.updateLockStatus('starting_docker');

  try {
    // First ensure Docker Desktop is running
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - please start Docker Desktop');
    }
    // ... rest of method
  }
}

## 1. Primary Request and Intent:

1. **Load session logs** (`/sl` command) for continuity from previous sessions

## 2. Key Technical Concepts:

- **Docker Mode Transition System**: Safe switching between native and Docker deployment modes with rollback capability
- **Process State Manager (PSM)**: Service registration and monitoring system
- **Health Monitoring with SIGUSR2/SIGUSR1**: Pause/resume signals for health monitors during transitions
- **Port binding conflicts**: Native services vs Docker containers competing for same ports
- **Container naming conventions**: Native mode uses `constraint-monitor-*`, `code-graph-rag-*` vs Docker compose uses `coding-*`
- **Docker Desktop auto-start on macOS**: Using `open -a "Docker"` and polling `docker ps`
- **Health check timeouts**: Docker `start_period: 120s` vs script timeout coordination

## 3. Files and Code Sections:

### `<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>cker-mode-transition.js`
**Why important**: This is the main file implementing the `--switch-to-docker` and `--switch-to-native` commands.

**Key additions:**

```javascript
// Health check timeout (must exceed Docker's start_period of 120s for coding-services)
const HEALTH_CHECK_TIMEOUT_MS = 150 * 1000;

// Docker startup timeout (wait for Docker Desktop to start)
const DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS = 45 * 1000;
```

```javascript
/**
 * Check if Docker daemon is ready (not just client)
 */
isDockerDaemonReady() {
  try {
    execSync('docker ps', { encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe' });
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Ensure Docker Desktop is running before attempting Docker operations
 * Mirrors the ensure_docker_running() logic from launch-claude.sh
 */
async ensureDockerRunning() {
  // Quick check if already running
  if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
    this.log('Docker daemon is already running');
    return true;
  }

  this.log('Docker daemon not running - attempting to start Docker Desktop...');

  // Check for stale Docker processes
  try {
    const psOutput = execSync('ps aux | grep -c "[c]om.docker.backend" || echo "0"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim();

    if (parseInt(psOutput) > 0) {
      this.log('Found stale Docker processes - force restarting...', 'warn');
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "Docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "com.docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      await this.sleep(2000);
    }
  } catch {
    // Ignore errors from ps/pkill
  }

  // Try to start Docker Desktop (macOS)
  const dockerAppPath = '/Applications/Docker.app';
  try {
    await fs.access(dockerAppPath);
  } catch {
    this.log('Docker Desktop not found at /Applications/Docker.app', 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Start Docker Desktop
  this.log('Starting Docker Desktop...');
  try {
    execSync('open -a "Docker"', { stdio: 'pipe' });
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Failed to launch Docker Desktop: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Wait for Docker daemon to become ready
  this.log(`Waiting for Docker daemon (max ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS / 1000} seconds)...`);
  const startTime = Date.now();

  while (Date.now() - startTime < DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS) {
    if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
      const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - startTime) / 1000);
      this.log(`Docker daemon ready after ${elapsed} seconds`);
      return true;
    }
    await this.sleep(1000);
  }

  this.log(`Docker daemon not ready after ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS/1000} seconds`, 'error');
  return false;
}
```

**Updated `servicesToStop` array:**
```javascript
const servicesToStop = [
  'system-health-dashboard-frontend',
  'system-health-dashboard-api',
  'vkb-server',
  'semantic-analysis-server',
  'constraint-monitor',
  'transcript-monitor',
  'live-logging-coordinator'
];
```

**Updated container stopping logic (BEFORE port killing):**
```javascript
// FIRST: Stop standalone Docker containers that may have been started by native mode services
if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
  this.log('Stopping standalone Docker containers from native mode...');

  const containerPatterns = [
    'constraint-monitor-',  // Redis, Qdrant from constraint monitor
    'code-graph-rag-',      // Memgraph, Lab from code-graph-rag
    'coding-'               // Any coding- prefixed containers
  ];

  try {
    const runningContainers = execSync('docker ps --format "{{.Names}}"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim().split('\n').filter(Boolean);

    for (const containerName of runningContainers) {
      if (containerPatterns.some(pattern => containerName.startsWith(pattern))) {
        this.log(`Stopping standalone container: ${containerName}...`);
        execSync(`docker stop ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe', timeout: 15000
        });
        execSync(`docker rm ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe'
        });
        this.log(`Stopped ${containerName}`);
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Warning: Could not list/stop containers: ${error.message}`, 'warn');
  }

  await this.sleep(2000);  // Give Docker time to release port bindings
}
```

**Updated port killing (only native ports):**
```javascript
// THEN: Release any remaining ports (non-Docker native processes)
const nativePorts = [

  3849,   // Constraint Monitor SSE

  }
}

/**
 * Ensure Docker Desktop is running before attempting Docker operations
 * Mirrors the ensure_docker_running() logic from launch-claude.sh

  // Quick check if already running

    this.log('Docker daemon is already running');
    return true;

  this.log('Docker daemon not running - attempting to start Docker Desktop...');

  // Check for stale Docker processes
  try {
    const psOutput = execSync('ps aux | grep -c "[c]om.docker.backend" || echo "0"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',

    if (parseInt(psOutput) > 0) {
      this.log('Found stale Docker processes - force restarting...', 'warn');
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "Docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "com.docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      await this.sleep(2000);
    }
  } catch {
    // Ignore errors from ps/pkill
  }

  // Try to start Docker Desktop (macOS)
  const dockerAppPath = '/Applications/Docker.app';
  try {
    await fs.access(dockerAppPath);
  } catch {
    this.log('Docker Desktop not found at /Applications/Docker.app', 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Start Docker Desktop
  this.log('Starting Docker Desktop...');
  try {
    execSync('open -a "Docker"', { stdio: 'pipe' });
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Failed to launch Docker Desktop: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Wait for Docker daemon to become ready
  this.log(`Waiting for Docker daemon (max ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS / 1000} seconds)...`);
  const startTime = Date.now();

  while (Date.now() - startTime < DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS) {
    if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
      const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - startTime) / 1000);
      this.log(`Docker daemon ready after ${elapsed} seconds`);
      return true;
    }
    await this.sleep(1000);
  }

  this.log(`Docker daemon not ready after ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS/1000} seconds`, 'error');
  return false;
}
```

**Updated `servicesToStop` array:**
```javascript
const servicesToStop = [
  'system-health-dashboard-frontend',
  'system-health-dashboard-api',
  'vkb-server',
  'semantic-analysis-server',
  'constraint-monitor',
  'transcript-monitor',
  'live-logging-coordinator'

**Updated container stopping logic (BEFORE port killing):**
```javascript
// FIRST: Stop standalone Docker containers that may have been started by native mode services
if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
  this.log('Stopping standalone Docker containers from native mode...');

  const containerPatterns = [
    'constraint-monitor-',  // Redis, Qdrant from constraint monitor
    'code-graph-rag-',      // Memgraph, Lab from code-graph-rag
    'coding-'               // Any coding- prefixed containers
  ];

  try {
    const runningContainers = execSync('docker ps --format "{{.Names}}"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim().split('\n').filter(Boolean);

    for (const containerName of runningContainers) {
      if (containerPatterns.some(pattern => containerName.startsWith(pattern))) {
        this.log(`Stopping standalone container: ${containerName}...`);
        execSync(`docker stop ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe', timeout: 15000
        });
        execSync(`docker rm ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe'
        });
        this.log(`Stopped ${containerName}`);
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Warning: Could not list/stop containers: ${error.message}`, 'warn');
  }

  await this.sleep(2000);  // Give Docker time to release port bindings
}
```

**Updated port killing (only native ports):**
```javascript
// THEN: Release any remaining ports (non-Docker native processes)
const nativePorts = [
  8080,   // VKB Server
  3032,   // Health Dashboard HTTP
  3033,   // Health Dashboard WebSocket
  3847,   // Browser Access SSE
  3848,   // Semantic Analysis SSE
  3849,   // Constraint Monitor SSE
  3850    // Code-Graph-RAG SSE
];
```

**Updated `transition()` method - early Docker check:**

try {

  if (targetMode === 'docker') {
    this.log('Ensuring Docker is available for transition...');
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - cannot proceed with transition');
    }
  }
  // ... rest of transition logic
}
```

**Updated `startDockerContainers()` - added Docker check:**
```javascript
async startDockerContainers() {
  this.log('Starting Docker containers...');
  await this.updateLockStatus('starting_docker');

  try {
    // First ensure Docker Desktop is running
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - please start Docker Desktop');
    }
    // ... rest of method
  }
}
```

## 2. Key Technical Concepts:

- **Docker Mode Transition System**: Safe switching between native and Docker deployment modes with rollback capability
- **Process State Manager (PSM)**: Service registration and monitoring system
- **Health Monitoring with SIGUSR2/SIGUSR1**: Pause/resume signals for health monitors during transitions
- **Port binding conflicts**: Native services vs Docker containers competing for same ports
- **Container naming conventions**: Native mode uses `constraint-monitor-*`, `code-graph-rag-*` vs Docker compose uses `coding-*`
- **Docker Desktop auto-start on macOS**: Using `open -a "Docker"` and polling `docker ps`
- **Health check timeouts**: Docker `start_period: 120s` vs script timeout coordination

### `<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>cker-mode-transition.js`
**Why important**: This is the main file implementing the `--switch-to-docker` and `--switch-to-native` commands.

**Key additions:**

```javascript
// Health check timeout (must exceed Docker's start_period of 120s for coding-services)
const HEALTH_CHECK_TIMEOUT_MS = 150 * 1000;

// Docker startup timeout (wait for Docker Desktop to start)
const DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS = 45 * 1000;
```

```javascript
/**
 * Check if Docker daemon is ready (not just client)
 */
isDockerDaemonReady() {
  try {
    execSync('docker ps', { encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe' });
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Ensure Docker Desktop is running before attempting Docker operations
 * Mirrors the ensure_docker_running() logic from launch-claude.sh
 */
async ensureDockerRunning() {
  // Quick check if already running
  if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
    this.log('Docker daemon is already running');
    return true;
  }

  this.log('Docker daemon not running - attempting to start Docker Desktop...');

  // Check for stale Docker processes
  try {
    const psOutput = execSync('ps aux | grep -c "[c]om.docker.backend" || echo "0"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim();

    if (parseInt(psOutput) > 0) {
      this.log('Found stale Docker processes - force restarting...', 'warn');
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "Docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "com.docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      await this.sleep(2000);
    }
  } catch {
    // Ignore errors from ps/pkill
  }

  // Try to start Docker Desktop (macOS)
  const dockerAppPath = '/Applications/Docker.app';
  try {
    await fs.access(dockerAppPath);
  } catch {
    this.log('Docker Desktop not found at /Applications/Docker.app', 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Start Docker Desktop
  this.log('Starting Docker Desktop...');
  try {
    execSync('open -a "Docker"', { stdio: 'pipe' });
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Failed to launch Docker Desktop: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Wait for Docker daemon to become ready
  this.log(`Waiting for Docker daemon (max ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS / 1000} seconds)...`);
  const startTime = Date.now();

  while (Date.now() - startTime < DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS) {
    if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
      const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - startTime) / 1000);
      this.log(`Docker daemon ready after ${elapsed} seconds`);
      return true;
    }
    await this.sleep(1000);
  }

  this.log(`Docker daemon not ready after ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS/1000} seconds`, 'error');
  return false;
}
```

   - Added `isDockerDaemonReady()` method using `docker ps`
   - Added `ensureDockerRunning()` method that starts Docker Desktop and waits up to 45s
   - Initially added this only to `startDockerContainers()` method

6. **First Test Failure**: Port 3033 already in use - System Health Dashboard services weren't being stopped

7. **Second Fix - Add Dashboard Services**:
   - Added `system-health-dashboard-frontend` and `system-health-dashboard-api` to `servicesToStop` array
   - Added them to `scriptPatterns` with their ports

8. **Second Test Failure**: Port 3100 (Memgraph Lab) in use - Native mode uses standalone Docker containers with different names

9. **Third Fix - Stop Standalone Containers**:
   - Added logic to stop containers matching patterns: `constraint-monitor-*`, `code-graph-rag-*`, `coding-*`

10. **Third Test Failure**: Port 6379 (Redis) still in use - Docker kept crashing because killing port processes killed container processes

11. **Fourth Fix - Reorder Operations**:
    - Moved Docker container stop BEFORE port killing
    - Only kill native service ports (8080, 3032, 3033, 3847-3850), not Docker-owned ports (6333, 6334, 6379, 7687, 3100)
    - Added check `if (this.isDockerDaemonReady())` before trying to stop containers

12. **Fifth Fix - Early Docker Start**:
    - Added `ensureDockerRunning()` call at the START of `transition()` method, before stopping native services
    - This ensures Docker is available to properly stop native mode containers

13. **Health Check Timeout Issue**: Containers started but health check timed out after 60s
    - Increased `HEALTH_CHECK_TIMEOUT_MS` from 60000 to 150000ms (150s vs Docker's 120s start_period)

14. **Docker Desktop Instability**: Docker Desktop kept crashing repeatedly during testing. Not a script issue but system stability issue.

15. **Final User Request**: "you do all of this for me: 1. Check Docker Desktop settings... 2. Check macOS Activity Monitor... 3. Check Docker Desktop logs... 4. Try resetting Docker Desktop... 5. Check for Docker updates"

- `<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>cker-mode-transition.js`

Summary:
## 1. Primary Request and Intent:

The user's primary requests were:
1. **Load session logs** (`/sl` command) for continuity from previous sessions
2. **Switch to full Docker mode** - but first fix the `--switch-to-docker` command to handle Docker Desktop not running. The script must automatically start Docker Desktop and ensure safe, robust transitions.
3. **Final request**: Investigate Docker Desktop stability issues by checking settings, Activity Monitor, logs, trying reset, and checking for updates.

## 2. Key Technical Concepts:

- **Docker Mode Transition System**: Safe switching between native and Docker deployment modes with rollback capability
- **Process State Manager (PSM)**: Service registration and monitoring system
- **Health Monitoring with SIGUSR2/SIGUSR1**: Pause/resume signals for health monitors during transitions
- **Port binding conflicts**: Native services vs Docker containers competing for same ports
- **Container naming conventions**: Native mode uses `constraint-monitor-*`, `code-graph-rag-*` vs Docker compose uses `coding-*`
- **Docker Desktop auto-start on macOS**: Using `open -a "Docker"` and polling `docker ps`
- **Health check timeouts**: Docker `start_period: 120s` vs script timeout coordination

## 3. Files and Code Sections:

### `<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>cker-mode-transition.js`
**Why important**: This is the main file implementing the `--switch-to-docker` and `--switch-to-native` commands.

**Key additions:**

```javascript
// Health check timeout (must exceed Docker's start_period of 120s for coding-services)
const HEALTH_CHECK_TIMEOUT_MS = 150 * 1000;

// Docker startup timeout (wait for Docker Desktop to start)
const DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS = 45 * 1000;
```

```javascript
/**
 * Check if Docker daemon is ready (not just client)
 */
isDockerDaemonReady() {
  try {
    execSync('docker ps', { encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe' });
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Ensure Docker Desktop is running before attempting Docker operations
 * Mirrors the ensure_docker_running() logic from launch-claude.sh
 */
async ensureDockerRunning() {
  // Quick check if already running
  if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
    this.log('Docker daemon is already running');
    return true;
  }

  this.log('Docker daemon not running - attempting to start Docker Desktop...');

  // Check for stale Docker processes
  try {
    const psOutput = execSync('ps aux | grep -c "[c]om.docker.backend" || echo "0"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim();

    if (parseInt(psOutput) > 0) {
      this.log('Found stale Docker processes - force restarting...', 'warn');
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "Docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      execSync('pkill -9 -f "com.docker" 2>/dev/null || true', { stdio: 'pipe' });
      await this.sleep(2000);
    }
  } catch {
    // Ignore errors from ps/pkill
  }

  // Try to start Docker Desktop (macOS)
  const dockerAppPath = '/Applications/Docker.app';
  try {
    await fs.access(dockerAppPath);
  } catch {
    this.log('Docker Desktop not found at /Applications/Docker.app', 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Start Docker Desktop
  this.log('Starting Docker Desktop...');
  try {
    execSync('open -a "Docker"', { stdio: 'pipe' });
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Failed to launch Docker Desktop: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    return false;
  }

  // Wait for Docker daemon to become ready
  this.log(`Waiting for Docker daemon (max ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS / 1000} seconds)...`);
  const startTime = Date.now();

  while (Date.now() - startTime < DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS) {
    if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
      const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - startTime) / 1000);
      this.log(`Docker daemon ready after ${elapsed} seconds`);
      return true;
    }
    await this.sleep(1000);
  }

  this.log(`Docker daemon not ready after ${DOCKER_STARTUP_TIMEOUT_MS/1000} seconds`, 'error');
  return false;
}
```

**Updated `servicesToStop` array:**
```javascript
const servicesToStop = [
  'system-health-dashboard-frontend',
  'system-health-dashboard-api',
  'vkb-server',
  'semantic-analysis-server',
  'constraint-monitor',
  'transcript-monitor',
  'live-logging-coordinator'
];
```

**Updated container stopping logic (BEFORE port killing):**
```javascript
// FIRST: Stop standalone Docker containers that may have been started by native mode services
if (this.isDockerDaemonReady()) {
  this.log('Stopping standalone Docker containers from native mode...');

  const containerPatterns = [
    'constraint-monitor-',  // Redis, Qdrant from constraint monitor
    'code-graph-rag-',      // Memgraph, Lab from code-graph-rag
    'coding-'               // Any coding- prefixed containers
  ];

  try {
    const runningContainers = execSync('docker ps --format "{{.Names}}"', {
      encoding: 'utf8',
      stdio: 'pipe'
    }).trim().split('\n').filter(Boolean);

    for (const containerName of runningContainers) {
      if (containerPatterns.some(pattern => containerName.startsWith(pattern))) {
        this.log(`Stopping standalone container: ${containerName}...`);
        execSync(`docker stop ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe', timeout: 15000
        });
        execSync(`docker rm ${containerName} 2>/dev/null || true`, {
          encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe'
        });
        this.log(`Stopped ${containerName}`);
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    this.log(`Warning: Could not list/stop containers: ${error.message}`, 'warn');
  }

  await this.sleep(2000);  // Give Docker time to release port bindings
}
```

**Updated port killing (only native ports):**
```javascript
// THEN: Release any remaining ports (non-Docker native processes)
const nativePorts = [
  8080,   // VKB Server
  3032,   // Health Dashboard HTTP
  3033,   // Health Dashboard WebSocket
  3847,   // Browser Access SSE
  3848,   // Semantic Analysis SSE
  3849,   // Constraint Monitor SSE
  3850    // Code-Graph-RAG SSE
];
```

**Updated `transition()` method - early Docker check:**
```javascript
try {
  // CRITICAL: If transitioning TO Docker, ensure Docker is running BEFORE stopping native services
  if (targetMode === 'docker') {
    this.log('Ensuring Docker is available for transition...');
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - cannot proceed with transition');
    }
  }
  // ... rest of transition logic
}
```

**Updated `startDockerContainers()` - added Docker check:**
```javascript
async startDockerContainers() {
  this.log('Starting Docker containers...');
  await this.updateLockStatus('starting_docker');

  try {
    // First ensure Docker Desktop is running
    const dockerReady = await this.ensureDockerRunning();
    if (!dockerReady) {
      throw new Error('Docker daemon is not available - please start Docker Desktop');
    }
    // ... rest of method
  }
}
```

## 4. Errors and Fixes:

1. **Port 3033 already in use (System Health Dashboard API)**
   - Fix: Added `system-health-dashboard-frontend` and `system-health-dashboard-api` to `servicesToStop` and `scriptPatterns`

2. **Port 3100 already in use (Memgraph Lab)**
   - Fix: Added logic to stop standalone containers matching patterns `constraint-monitor-*`, `code-graph-rag-*`

3. **Port 6379 already in use (Redis) - Docker crashing**
   - Root cause: Killing processes on Docker-owned ports was killing container processes, confusing Docker
   - Fix: Moved container stopping BEFORE port killing; only kill native service ports, not Docker-owned ports

4. **Docker daemon not available during `stopNativeServices()`**
   - Root cause: Docker check happened too late
   - Fix: Added `ensureDockerRunning()` call at START of `transition()` method

5. **Health check timeout after 60s**
   - Root cause: Docker's `start_period: 120s` > script's 60s timeout
   - Fix: Increased `HEALTH_CHECK_TIMEOUT_MS` from 60000 to 150000ms

6. **Docker Desktop repeatedly crashing**
   - Status: UNRESOLVED - Docker Desktop stability issue on user's machine, not script issue

## 5. Problem Solving:

**Solved:**
- Docker auto-start logic implemented
- Proper ordering of operations (containers before ports)
- Correct identification of which ports are Docker-owned vs native
- Extended health check timeouts

**Ongoing:**
- Docker Desktop stability - keeps crashing during operations (system issue, not script issue)
